<div id="review_1273756206" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1273756206" />
    <a title="Andie " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30510075-andie"><img alt="Andie " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1477111902p2/30510075.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1273756206?book_show_action=true">May 06, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Andie " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Andie " href="/user/show/30510075-andie">Andie </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30510075-andie?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30510075-andie?shelf=dystopian">dystopian</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1273756206" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7569684017513489472"><b> Spoilers have been tagged but if you've read my review of THE HEIR, the outcome of THE CROWN will be spoiled nonetheless. </b> <br/><br/>2.5 stars<br/><br/>Disappointed is an understatement. Where's the romance?! <br/><br/>As a huge fan of The Selection trilogy, I was ecstatic when Kiera gave us 'The Heir' as a spinoff story. I was really disappointed with Eadlyn's characterization but she showed room for growth and I prayed she would get it together in 'The Crown'. While she did surprise me and do an almost complete 180, it ju</span>
  <span id="freeText7569684017513489472" style="display:none"><b> Spoilers have been tagged but if you've read my review of THE HEIR, the outcome of THE CROWN will be spoiled nonetheless. </b> <br /><br />2.5 stars<br /><br />Disappointed is an understatement. Where's the romance?! <br /><br />As a huge fan of The Selection trilogy, I was ecstatic when Kiera gave us 'The Heir' as a spinoff story. I was really disappointed with Eadlyn's characterization but she showed room for growth and I prayed she would get it together in 'The Crown'. While she did surprise me and do an almost complete 180, it just wasn't enough for me. And here's why - my SHIP completely sunk! <br /><br />I, like many others, was rooting for <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Kile  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> from the very beginning. Eadlyn's choice makes ZERO sense to me. It was never clear if she felt something for this guy or not and then after one specific conversation she decides SOULMATES! He doesn't really become a competitor until about the last 1/4 of the book. It was completely out of the blue and I didn't much care for it. <br /><br />The obvious choice was <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Kile  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> in my opinion. They had more chemistry than any of the other boys. In fact, I felt a complete disconnect from all but two of the boys (her choice is not included in the two). <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ There's something about childhood friends turning lovers that's just so appealing  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> maybe it's predictable but it's the fairytale story that I was hoping to see unfold - watching them go from not caring much for the other to falling in love. Because isn't that what The Selection was originally about? I feel cheated! <br /><br />Besides the lack of romance, the entirety of the book felt rushed, even more so at the end. Can the epilogue even be called an epilogue? Ugh I'm just so disappointed that after a year of waiting for the series conclusion this book ended up feeling like an after thought. <br /><br />What I DID like:<br /><br />-Eadlyn goes from being a snotty brat in The Heir to a strong, caring, down to earth girl. <br />-Maxon and America. Thank god they were here to remind us what true love is. <br /><br />I can't think of anything else I really enjoyed. Such a shame because I love Kiera Cass as an author. </span>
  <a data-text-id="7569684017513489472" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer5358080231138061159"><b>
  <u>5 Absolutely Fantastic ★'s</u>
</b> <br/><br/><i>"I had power and no idea how to use it. I was a ruler who didn’t know how to lead. I was a twin who was on her own. I was a daughter with missing parents. I had a half dozen suitors and wasn’t sure how to be in love. "</i><br/><blockquote>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1545015489i/26757809.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</blockquote> <br/><i>“It was a delicious feeling, falling in love. I'd had so many luxuries in my life, and I thought I'd had a taste of this before, but I realized now it was merely a cheap imitation of something not meant to be imitated in the first place.”</i> <br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1545018307i/26758171.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1543275640i/26652408._SX540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Buddy r</span>
  <span id="freeText5358080231138061159" style="display:none"><b>
  <u>5 Absolutely Fantastic ★'s</u>
</b> <br><br><i>"I had power and no idea how to use it. I was a ruler who didn’t know how to lead. I was a twin who was on her own. I was a daughter with missing parents. I had a half dozen suitors and wasn’t sure how to be in love. "</i><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1545015489i/26757809.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote> <br><i>“It was a delicious feeling, falling in love. I'd had so many luxuries in my life, and I thought I'd had a taste of this before, but I realized now it was merely a cheap imitation of something not meant to be imitated in the first place.”</i> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1545018307i/26758171.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1543275640i/26652408._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Buddy read with my, girl <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/86233338-desire-lambert" rel="nofollow noopener">Desireé</a> :) <br><br><u>Reread</u><br><br>There are a lot of differences in opinions when it comes to <i>The Selection</i> series. I for one fall on the side that is in LOVE with it! This series is AMAZING and these books are golden. They are light fluffy wonderful goodness. <i>The Selection</i> series is the perfect books to read when I need a break from the heavy, epic, giant, books I read a lot of. I know this series has been over since <i>2016</i> but still, I am so sad that it's over. <br><br>As for <i>The Crown</i>, It. Was. Marvelous!! I love the beginning the middle and the end. So yeah, you could say I love the WHOLE damn book. It was just perfect! Just like all the rest once I opened the book I was unable to put it down. I couldn't devour each sentence each chapter fast enough. And though some things were pretty predictable, I enjoyed it immensely. I thought the writing was beautifully rendered and at times I found that I had the most ridiculous grin on my face. I couldn't help but smile. Still, as I'm writing this review I can't help smiling thinking back on all that has happened. I absolutely love all the sweet, cheesy and endearing moments. This was truly lovely, I just really wish this final book would have been a LOT longer because it really was too short :( But the Conclusion was really wonderful and swoony and it didn't disappoint whatsoever. There is enough drama, intrigue and heart filled scenes to satisfy and <i>Kiera Cass</i> sure knows how to mess with my feelings and pull at my heartstrings and she does so brilliantly especially in this book. The love these characters have for one another is intense and it makes me very emotional. I cried off and on throughout the last half and I thought my heart might explode from happiness. I adored Eadlyn in <i>The Heir</i> but I think I love her even more in <i>The Crown</i> because of the growth of Eadlyn's character. She grows so much and though she keeps her fiery spirit it's more refined and controlled. Eadlyn really grows into herself, being around all those boys from all different backgrounds of life changed her in so many ways. From the way, she sees herself to the world around her. I love so many of the guys but my favorites are Eikko, Kile, Henri, Hale, Fox and Ian and in that order. They are all wonderful and were such a joy to get to know and love. I am super happy with who Eadlyn ends up with... I KNEW it would be him and I truly couldn't be any more ecstatic with the outcome! <b>#TeamEikko</b> Forever &amp; Always!!! I love this book, this series, this world more than I can ever express and I find such contentment in the way it has ended. I recommend this series to anyone looking for something light and sweet and full of funny, happy and cheesy goodness :D <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1543275640i/26652408._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>“Maybe it's not the first kisses that are supposed to be special. Maybe it's the last ones.”</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1545031173i/26759061.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1543275640i/26652408._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>*This audiobook was perfect! Agan... Brittany Pressley (the Narrator), did an incredible job. If you are an audiobook lover then you don't miss this one :D Also, the cover is gorgeous, I love it!! :)*</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1543275640i/26652408._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He smiled. <b>
  <i>“You are always just Eadlyn. And you are always the queen. You are everything to everyone. And infinitely more to me.”</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>“The world woke up when I looked at him.”</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>“I pulled him to me. Kissing him as if our lives depended on it.”</i>
</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1545037134ra/26759339.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>“I'd wondered how it was possible to magically find a soul mate in a random group of boys. But now I couldn't question it.”</i><br><br><i>I looked over, and something in his expression, the hopefulness in his eyes, calmed me. I forgot the cameras. <b>“As such, I've fallen hopelessly in love with him.”</b></i><br><br><b>
  <i>“And I you,”</i>
</b> he answered so quietly, no one may have even noticed.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5358080231138061159" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1257490285" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1257490285" />
    <a title="NiCoLeTa E. {Addicted To Books}" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/37314676-nicoleta-e-addicted-to-books"><img alt="NiCoLeTa E. {Addicted To Books}" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1528808758p2/37314676.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1257490285?book_show_action=true">Apr 17, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="NiCoLeTa E. {Addicted To Books}" class="user" itemprop="url" name="NiCoLeTa E. {Addicted To Books}" href="/user/show/37314676-nicoleta-e-addicted-to-books">NiCoLeTa E. {Addicted To Books}</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/26150713-the-crown">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/37314676-nicoleta-e-addicted-to-books?shelf=fairytales">fairytales</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/37314676-nicoleta-e-addicted-to-books?shelf=romance-young-adult-etc">romance-young-adult-etc</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1257490285" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8711743631452706411"><b>
  <i>***4 "<u>Happily Ever After</u>" stars***</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462625235ra/19022516.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>“Trust your gut. Trust your heart.”<br/>“I’m terrified of my heart.” I didn’t mean to say those words out loud, but there was something about him that made this room, and this moment, the only place I could ever admit to the truth.<br/>He leaned down by my ear and whispered, “There’s nothing there to fear.” </i>
</b><br/><br/>I'm a sucker for fairy tales...<br/>And i was almost obsessed with the first three parts of the series...<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462625235ra/19022517.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>America and Maxon were amazing and i will never forget thei</span>
  <span id="freeText8711743631452706411" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>***4 "<u>Happily Ever After</u>" stars***</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462625235ra/19022516.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>“Trust your gut. Trust your heart.”<br>“I’m terrified of my heart.” I didn’t mean to say those words out loud, but there was something about him that made this room, and this moment, the only place I could ever admit to the truth.<br>He leaned down by my ear and whispered, “There’s nothing there to fear.” </i>
</b><br><br>I'm a sucker for fairy tales...<br>And i was almost obsessed with the first three parts of the series...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462625235ra/19022517.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>America and Maxon were amazing and i will never forget their story...<br><i>And then came Eadlyn and everything changed...</i><br><br><b>
  <i>"Seriously, even if I did find someone, could it ever compare to them?"</i>
</b><br><br>The fourth book wasn't my favorite... Eadlyn was America and Maxon's only daughter and she had nothing from the brightness of her parents...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387604492ra/7628266.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>She was spoiled, she had a great opinion of herself and she was sooooo annoying...<br><i>But damn, i needed to find out with whom she will end up...</i><br><br><b>
  <i>"I was surrounded by examples of how love, real love, could make you less bothered by your circumstances, whether it was facing the greatest disappointment of your life or shouldering the weight of a country. And suddenly, for the life of me, I couldn’t remember why I’d been so afraid of it.<br>I mentally thumbed through my list of suitors. Kile’s sweetness, Fox’s enthusiasm, Henri’s joy … these were all things that drew me in. But, beyond that, was there something beautiful and lasting?<br>I still didn’t know. But finding out no longer looked so frightening."</i>
</b><br><br>In my heart, i wanted her to end up with one of two candidates....<br>And to be honest while i started this book, i diminished them to one....<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443469132ra/16363612.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>And yep, i'm so happy because my wish came true after all!!!<br><i>Nope, sorry guys, i can't tell you who he was!!!</i><br><br><b>
  <i>"No, this whole process made no sense, but I could see how it happened, how your heart could get swept up in the endeavor. And that was my hope now: that somehow duty and love would overlap, and I’d find myself happy in the middle of it all."</i>
</b><br><br>The blissful thing in this story is that Eadlyn had changed... a lot!!!<br>She wasn't annoying anymore and you could say that she was more approachable... and i liked this change... <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462625235ra/19022518.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>The snob and selfish girl had vanished and in her place were a lovely, full of grace girl...<br><i>Thank God!!!</i><br><br><b>
  <i>"I had power and no idea how to use it. I was a ruler who didn’t know how to lead. I was a twin who was on her own. I was a daughter with missing parents. I had a half dozen suitors and wasn’t sure how to be in love."</i>
</b><br><br>Αfter the flight of her twin and her mother's unexpected illness, Eadlyn had to grow up...<br>She stepped into her father's shoes temporary and she had lots to deal... and mostly her people's disbelief in her face...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462625235ra/19022519.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>And except all the above, she had to continue with the Selection and the six remaining men, the Elite...<br><i>But what will happen when the cold hearted girl will start to fall in love with someone that she can't have????</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462625235ra/19022520.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>“This will be the first time in my life I haven’t been able to have something I truly wanted. It’s so cruel that it happens to be you.”</i>
</b><br><br><i>No, i can't tell you more!!!</i><br>The only thing that i will say is that as a very sensitive person, my heart was breaking with the torment of Eadlyn's heart near to the end... <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462625236ra/19022521.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Seriously, i couldn't stop the tears and i am so embarrassed for that!!!<br>But i have to say that i enjoyed this book, especially the last half...<br><br><b>
  <i>"I had felt it growing, this feeling that had been hiding beneath the surface for some time now. I’d seen him, this person who never intended to be seen, and my faulty, silly, useless heart kept whispering his name. I clutched my chest, feeling my heart racing. “You treacherous, treacherous thing. What have you done?”<br>I’d wondered how it was possible to magically find a soul mate in a random group of boys.<br>But now I couldn’t question it."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462556024ra/19013912.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="8711743631452706411" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1434747586" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1434747586" />
    <a title="Dana Kenedy (Dana and the Books)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/372001-dana-kenedy-dana-and-the-books"><img alt="Dana Kenedy (Dana and the Books)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1464902542p2/372001.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1434747586?book_show_action=true">Nov 05, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dana Kenedy (Dana and the Books)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dana Kenedy (Dana and the Books)" href="/user/show/372001-dana-kenedy-dana-and-the-books">Dana Kenedy (Dana and the Books)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/372001-dana-kenedy-dana-and-the-books?shelf=netgalley">netgalley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/372001-dana-kenedy-dana-and-the-books?shelf=2016-release">2016-release</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/372001-dana-kenedy-dana-and-the-books?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/372001-dana-kenedy-dana-and-the-books?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/372001-dana-kenedy-dana-and-the-books?shelf=read-in-2016">read-in-2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/372001-dana-kenedy-dana-and-the-books?shelf=arc">arc</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1434747586" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7412774843642088449">This review can also be found <a href='http://danaandthebooks.com/2016/07/12/review-the-crown/' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>on my blog, Dana and the Books</a>.<br/><br/>The Selection series is my guilty pleasure.<br/><br/>If you've never read the series, it's essentially The Bachelor/The Bachelorette set in a dystopian future and with royalty.  I also suggest you stop reading this review if you haven't read the series as there are spoilers for the first four books here.<br/><br/><em>The Heir </em>(Book #4) takes place twenty years after the first three books and we find ourselves thrust into another selection.  Except this time t</span>
  <span id="freeText7412774843642088449" style="display:none">This review can also be found <a href="http://danaandthebooks.com/2016/07/12/review-the-crown/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">on my blog, Dana and the Books</a>.<br /><br />The Selection series is my guilty pleasure.<br /><br />If you've never read the series, it's essentially The Bachelor/The Bachelorette set in a dystopian future and with royalty.  I also suggest you stop reading this review if you haven't read the series as there are spoilers for the first four books here.<br /><br /><em>The Heir </em>(Book #4) takes place twenty years after the first three books and we find ourselves thrust into another selection.  Except this time the girl chooses from a group of boys.  The girl, Eadlyn, is of course the daughter of America and Maxon—the subjects of the first three books.<br /><br /><em>The Crown </em>(Book #5) picks up where <em>The Heir</em> ends: right after we find out America has had a shocking heart attack and then follows Eadlyn to the end of The Selection.<br /><br />Yes, the whole premise of this series is totally corny and there isn't anything spectacular about the actual writing itself, but it's so adorable and addictive. It's kind of like watching bad reality TV, you know it's bad, but you keep looking for more because you enjoy it on some strange level.<br /><br />Overall, I did find it a great conclusion to the series. It was definitely predictable, but I think if Kiera Cass ended it any other way it wouldn't have worked, and I would have walked away feeling like all the time I put into reading this series was a waste.<br /><br />All of the books in the series are quick reads, but I found I got through <em>The Crown</em> much faster than the others.  It was <em>very</em> short: 278 pages. To put that into perspective, the four other books are all more than 300 pages.  Since this was the last book <em>and</em> it was so short, it felt rushed.<br /><br />I like who she ends up with but I wish we had more build up and a longer look at the relationships between all of the guys who were left in <em>The Crown</em>.  Again, I feel this final book was far too short for a series closer. I wanted more side plots, more tension, more of a conclusion.<br /><br />Yes, these five books have been drawn out when it really could have been just three, but I don't care. I want more.<br /><br />I want to experience another Selection.<br /><br />Thanks so much to HarperCollins UK Children's for approving me for a copy on Netgalley!<br /><br />Pick up your own copy (<a href="http://amzn.to/2a59gxl" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon US</a> / <a href="http://www.amazon.ca/gp/product/0062458868/ref=as_li_ss_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=15121&amp;creative=390961&amp;creativeASIN=0062458868&amp;linkCode=as2&amp;tag=danandthebo07-20" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon CA</a> / <a href="http://www.anrdoezrs.net/links/7919222/type/dlg/https://www.chapters.indigo.ca/en-ca/books/the-crown/9780062458865-item.html?ikwid=the+crown&amp;ikwsec=Home&amp;ikwidx=0" rel="nofollow noopener">Indigo</a> /<a href="http://www.bookdepository.com/The-Crown-Kier-Cass/9780007580248/?a_aid=DanaAndTheBooks" rel="nofollow noopener"> Book Depository</a>)!</span>
  <a data-text-id="7412774843642088449" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1499302545" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7733229900356689544"><u>EDIT</u>: Apparently there might be a <a href='http://deadline.com/2015/04/the-selection-keira-cass-katie-lovejoy-warner-bros-1201413855/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Selection Movie</a> coming up soon?<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1466779416ra/19519270.gif' height='120' width='350' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>(Actual Review)<br/>I would say I'm disappointed but that's a lie. I totally expected this book to have 0 literary worth. The only reason I even read this series is that a certain friend pressured me into it every step of the way. <br/><br/>So Eadlyn is still hated by her citizens because she's a shallow, self-absorbed child. To raise her public ratings her family decides to marry her off to a worthy suitor, because seeing Eadlyn happy will regai</span>
  <span id="freeText7733229900356689544" style="display:none"><u>EDIT</u>: Apparently there might be a <a href="http://deadline.com/2015/04/the-selection-keira-cass-katie-lovejoy-warner-bros-1201413855/" rel="nofollow noopener">Selection Movie</a> coming up soon?<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1466779416ra/19519270.gif" height="120" width="350" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>(Actual Review)<br>I would say I'm disappointed but that's a lie. I totally expected this book to have 0 literary worth. The only reason I even read this series is that a certain friend pressured me into it every step of the way. <br><br>So Eadlyn is still hated by her citizens because she's a shallow, self-absorbed child. To raise her public ratings her family decides to marry her off to a worthy suitor, because seeing Eadlyn happy will regain the country's support. (On a side note, when I see someone I despise in a happy mood, it makes me want to strangle them. So why exactly would this plan work?) In any case, everything goes wrong because Eadlyn manages to fall for the one and only guy in the castle who isn't trying to put a ring on it. Good going there. <br><br>Besides the shallowness and narrow-mindedness and egotism, Eadlyn is an awful role model. When she's self-confident, she shows it by putting other people down (she especially likes to make fun of poor people). And the rest of the time she's ridiculously insecure. For example, one guy tells her he can't marry her because he doesn't swing that way, and her immediate response is:<br><i>"This was my worst fear coming to life. I was unlovable. I knew it."</i><br>I CANNOT BELIEVE this girl. I really hope there aren't any impressionable young ladies taking lessons from Eadlyn's behavior. <br><br>So glad this series is over and can't plague me anymore. DOBBY IS A FREE ELF</span>

<div id="review_1088291019" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1088291019" />
    <a title="Sarah Elizabeth" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7591340-sarah-elizabeth"><img alt="Sarah Elizabeth" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1328957304p2/7591340.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1088291019?book_show_action=true">Oct 24, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sarah Elizabeth" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sarah Elizabeth" href="/user/show/7591340-sarah-elizabeth">Sarah Elizabeth</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/27829330-the-crown">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7591340-sarah-elizabeth?shelf=dystopian">dystopian</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7591340-sarah-elizabeth?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7591340-sarah-elizabeth?shelf=love-triangle">love-triangle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7591340-sarah-elizabeth?shelf=netgalley-edelweiss">netgalley-edelweiss</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7591340-sarah-elizabeth?shelf=r2r-read">r2r-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7591340-sarah-elizabeth?shelf=read-2016">read-2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7591340-sarah-elizabeth?shelf=as">as</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7591340-sarah-elizabeth?shelf=read-with-abbie">read-with-abbie</a>,

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1088291019" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14645291561089426243">(Source: I received a digital copy of this book for free on a read-to-review basis. Thanks to HarperCollins UK Children's, and NetGalley.)<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“There were things I was always sure of, and almost all of that has fallen apart in the last few weeks.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1460913639i/18804219.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This was a good end to the series, and Eadlyn really played her role well.<br/><br/>Eadlyn continued to be a strong character in this book; she really stepped up, she put others first, and she really cared about what was good for everyone else rather than </span>
  <span id="freeText14645291561089426243" style="display:none">(Source: I received a digital copy of this book for free on a read-to-review basis. Thanks to HarperCollins UK Children's, and NetGalley.)<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“There were things I was always sure of, and almost all of that has fallen apart in the last few weeks.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1460913639i/18804219.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This was a good end to the series, and Eadlyn really played her role well.<br><br>Eadlyn continued to be a strong character in this book; she really stepped up, she put others first, and she really cared about what was good for everyone else rather than just for her, which was quite an improvement.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I know it’s abrupt, but given my mother’s precarious condition, my father has asked me to take on more responsibilities.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1460913639i/18804220._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The storyline in this was about Eadlyn stepping up following her mother’s illness, and taking on a role that she was young for, but capable of it seemed. We also had the culmination of the Selection, but there wasn’t quite as much of the storyline devoted to this as I expected, and the book felt more about Eadlyn stepping up than about the romance.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I feel the only way to manage that is to scale down this competition.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1460913639i/18804221._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>With regards to the romance, it really did seem to be missing from the majority of this book, and then Eadlyn made some very strange decisions, and I really didn’t get what she was doing! The person who I expected her to be with by the end just didn’t happen, and I wasn’t 100% sure about the person she eventually chose.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I can’t just kiss you like it’s nothing, because it turns out that you’re not nothing.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1460913639i/18804222.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The ending to this wrapped things up nicely, and we did get a happily ever after, it just wasn’t quite what I expected.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“The truth is, love is as much fate as it is planning, as much beauty as it is disaster.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1460913639i/18804223.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>8 out of 10</span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35614518-chesca-thecrownedpages?shelf=read-in-2016">read-in-2016</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35614518-chesca-thecrownedpages?shelf=dystopia">dystopia</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35614518-chesca-thecrownedpages?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1245642519" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6375985996905063847"><i>
  <b>“Maybe it's not the first kisses that are supposed to be special. Maybe it's the last ones.”</b>
</i><br/><br/><b>Actual Rating: 4.5 stars</b><br/><br/>OH. EM. GEE.<br/><br/>I JUST FINISHED THE CROWN AND I CAN’T KEEP CALM!!!<br/><br/>I’ve been reading mixed reviews about this last installment of The Selection by Kiera Cass, so I was so nervous to start it and to finish it. But guess what I feel after reading it? I AM SO HAPPY I was literally crying as I was finishing the book. I was not disappointed that much except by a few parts.<br/><br/>What I really l</span>
  <span id="freeText6375985996905063847" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>“Maybe it's not the first kisses that are supposed to be special. Maybe it's the last ones.”</b>
</i><br /><br /><b>Actual Rating: 4.5 stars</b><br /><br />OH. EM. GEE.<br /><br />I JUST FINISHED THE CROWN AND I CAN’T KEEP CALM!!!<br /><br />I’ve been reading mixed reviews about this last installment of The Selection by Kiera Cass, so I was so nervous to start it and to finish it. But guess what I feel after reading it? I AM SO HAPPY I was literally crying as I was finishing the book. I was not disappointed that much except by a few parts.<br /><br />What I really like about <i>
  <b>The Crown</b>
</i> is that the characters and their relationships have been well developed. I have loved each and every one of them until the very last page. Yes, even Josie whom I loathed so much before that I almost wished for another massacre in the palace just to get her out of the picture.<br /><br />There were also a lot of things revealed about Maxon and America, things we never knew about them before. The two of them are really admirable and I would miss them. They are one of the best fictional parents and couples ever written. I could say that they got better and better from what I’ve seen in them from the very first book.<br /><br />We also got to know more about The Elite and I was really surprised about those facts. I’m really glad for them all, especially Kile, Hale, and Ean. I want to hug the three of them.<br /><br />I am really happy that Eadlyn ended up with… one of the guys I was shipping. I really knew that they could be the one for each other since I was reading the previous book. I sure am going to have a happy book-hangover after this.<br /><br />What didn’t work for me, first, is how the coronation part was written. The reasons for it were not enough for me. It was really sweet, yes, but it was kind of mishandled, and showed a bit of irresponsibility from the other characters. I could say that it was too abrupt. The second one is the Epilogue. It was so short, and the words written in it could have been placed in the author’s Acknowledgements!! Those were such lovely words but it won’t satisfy anyone. Lastly, I wasn’t that happy with how the ending was written. I am really glad of how it ended, I swear, it’s just that it wasn’t that grand. I want a very unforgettable ending not a simple one! I think this series deserved a better closing than that.<br /><br />Overall, this series is going to be remembered. If you asked me as I was reading the first three books if I love this series, I would say that I don't love it that much. Now, I could say that I really do. It proved that love is imperfect but it’s us who make it beautiful. Sometimes it’s all about perspective, as one of the characters has said. You just have to learn to look at the right place, at the right angle, to find what you’re looking for.<br /><br />Now, I should go back to my corner and cry my eyes out. I will really miss this series.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6375985996905063847" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground">Readers also enjoyed</h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent"><div class='bookCarousel'>
<div class='carouselRow' style='width: 3600px'>
<ul>
<li class='cover' id='bookCover_23174274'>
<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23174274-glass-sword"><img alt="Glass Sword (Red Queen, #2)" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1436460934l/23174274._SX98_.jpg" />
</a>

  
<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Jsx8YnjmAIdFd02uN4xnrgZ4vJTd65wfBmof8Y/yi6gtepZArl8WkiQF6REeVcwgjrNICj40PLQ7ji1xdmYa4w==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('vFyxv8f51jF3bueWT3g1+5w1wGgusmFDH2fl8UBcBrW36ludEUDAJBYcQylmoZ51FP409s1twegig9dxuciX/g==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

Doing things alone. Getting real mail. Decorating. Small forks. A good hug. Gift cards. New Years Goals. Going out to dinner. When someone else remembers some great story about me/us that I’ve forgotten. Toy stores. Fireplaces. Breakfast foods. Journaling. Crying for a good reason. Doorbells. Pointless adventures. Voting.
